The last time I was there, I had a couple of aged cacha\u00e7a shots and a tangerine Caipirinha. It was delicious. \n\nThe apetizers are typically the same, I doubt they change that menu. My favorite little dish is called  Escondidinho, a yukka pureed small dish filled with beef jerky, au gratin, served in little ramekins and many times shared between two friends,  perhaps because the concoction is too rich for one person, or perhaps because sharing dishes brings proximity and better conversations. This particular Academia (as locals call it) is in the Leblon neighborhood, and most of the tables are set outside the small restaurant.
